â€œAre Prisoners Who Have Their Hearts Removed for Transplantation Actually Dead?â€ While it has been proven by other researchers that Falun Gong practitioners and Uyghur Muslims are the two main groups targeted in organ harvesting, Lavee and Robertson still questioned whether donors were actually dead when the doctors removed their hearts.  As they wrote in the Tablet article: â€œFor an organ donor to be medically and legally dead, brain or circulatory death must first be declared. Brain death is the permanent and irreversible cessation of all brain function, including breathing. As long as ventilation is artificially maintained in such patients, the heart continues to beat for a short while, thus keeping vital organs viable and suitable for transplantation.  â€œThis question is central, because if the prisoner donors in China were indeed brain dead at the time, then heart extraction would not have been the cause of death. But if the declaration of brain death was falseâ€”or indeed, medically impossibleâ€”then heart procurement would necessarily have been the cause of death. In other words, the prisoners would have been alive at the time of heart extraction and the surgeons would have been executioners.â€  To answer their question, they searched 120,000 Chinese-language medical publications in both academic and medical databases from the 1950s to late 2020, using keywords such as â€œè„‘æ­»äº¡åç«‹å³æ°”ç®¡å†…æ’ç®¡ç»™æ°§â€(â€œafter brain death, immediately perform endotracheal intubationâ€) and â€œä¾›ä½“å¤§è„‘æ­»äº¡å,é¦–å…ˆåˆ†ç§’å¿…äº‰åœ°å»ºç«‹å‘¼å¸ä¸é™è„‰é€šé“â€(â€œafter donor brain death, race against the clock to establish respiratory and venous accessâ€).  In their findings, there were 71 studies published between 1980 and 2015 that concerned 56 hospitals, including 12 military hospitals, in 33 cities across 15 provinces. These studies indicated that brain death was not properly declared before the heart extraction. Thus, the transplant itself was the cause of the donorâ€™s death.  Lavee and Robertson cited one such study (which they coded as paper 0191) in the appendix of the AJT paper. This study stated that the Chinese surgeon involved in the transplant made it very clear that the victimâ€™s heart was still beating before they removed it. â€œThe donor was intravenously injected with heparin 3mg/kg 1h before the operation â€¦ The heartbeat was weak and the myocardium was purple. After assisted ventilation through tracheal intubation, the myocardium turned red and the heartbeat turned strong â€¦ The donor heart was extracted with an incision from the 4th intercostal sternum â€¦ This incision is a good choice for field operation where the sternum cannot be sawed open without power.â€  In another study that Lavee and Robertson coded as paper 0173, another Chinese surgeon admitted that the victim was still breathing and not intubated. â€œBefore the chest is opened, 100mg of heparin is injected and the mask is pressurized to give oxygen to assist breathing.â€  A third study coded as paper 0463 said that a surgeon revealed an important detail: â€œAfter the donor is confirmed brain dead, four cases of tracheal intubation, three cases of mask oxygenation, quickly establish artificial respiration, rapid median thoracic dissection â€¦â€ If the victim was already dead, they wouldnâ€™t have been able to breathe on their own and the (oxygen) mask wouldnâ€™t have been necessary. When the surgeon still used the (oxygen) mask on the victims, the only possibility was that they were still breathing and alive.
